Journal of Life Sciences: Proceedings

Available online 27 January 2024
In Press, Corrected ProofWhat’s this?

A Review on the first year of married life of aspiring PhD couple

Author links open overlay panel,
https://doi.org/10.1016/j.matpr.2023.02.036Get rights and content

Abstract

The present study attempts to review the significance of important incidents, the feelings induced and the outpour of emotions in the first year of married life of the authors. The paper studies in detail about the incidents leading up to the marriage and the events that unfolded in the months following the marriage. The incidents have been reviewed along with pertinent images to induce a similar feeling when reading about the incident and to give a small taste of numerous cherishable memories that the authors have built together. The review of the events from the "memory journal" lead to the conclusion that the authors love each other like crazy and they chose to work on their marriage in spite of the numerous verbal battles they had faced. The study also found that there is a high possibility of the author living together for another fifty years in happiness, cherishing their memories together.

Introduction

The married couples have always yearned for a healthier marriage life as evident from many testimonies. One of the major focal points being addressed in order to achieve this outcome is the periodic review of the said married couple's past experiences. The methodologies that are frontiers in achieving this purpose include sharing reels, old photos and journaling. All of these methodologies are based on the premise that being grateful about good times and learning from your mistakes always lead to a better life.

The current study is a review of the first year of marriage, the good, the bad, the overwhelming laughter and cries that the authors have experienced. The aim of this study is to express the love and affection that one author has on his better half.

Section snippets

Photographs

For the explicit purpose of analysing the magnitude of the significance of the memories of the first year on the health of the married life, the methodology to review the photographs has been proposed. This involves reviewing the photographs from the first meet [1] till the recent aquarium visit at Tambaram. [10]

Description of Memories

For the explicit purpose of evoking the similar feelings that the authors felt during these moments captured by the photographs, a short passage outlining the thought process of the authors have also been included. These passages include the authors excitement during the train ride to see his future better half[1], his hesitation,doubt and eventual happiness before and after sending his first text[2]. The memories reviewed here are those that have been recorded via photographs and texts a few of the memories may not be described in detail.

Conclusion

The present study explored the significance of the memories and the feelings of the author on the health of the marriage. The photographs revealed that the authors have had a healthy relationship filled with intimacy, travel and a lot of love. The review of the said memories also revealed an astounding fact that the authors grew even closer to each others hearts after a big fight. This increase in intimacy resulted in the love they had for each other.
